                function showBangVangT3(tuan)
                {
                    $.ajax({
                            type: "GET",
                            url: "//vuachoibai.com/event/BangVang2016T3/MainPopup?week="+tuan,
                            success: function (data) {
                                ChumTaXi2015.ShowPopup(data, 750, 500);
                                $("#popupwrap2").draggable();
                                $("#scrollMiniEvent").mCustomScrollbar({autoHideScrollbar: true});
                            }
                        });
                }   
                function showChiTietBangVangT3(tuan, page)
                {
                    $.ajax({
                            type: "GET",
                            url: "//vuachoibai.com/event/BangVang2016T3/Details?week="+tuan+"&currPage="+page,
                            success: function (data) {
                                ChumTaXi2015.ShowPopup(data, 750, 500);
                                $("#popupwrap2").draggable();
                                $("#scrollMiniEvent").mCustomScrollbar({autoHideScrollbar: true});
                            }
                        });
                }
                function ShowVipPointEvent()
                {
                    $("#BVVipPoint").show();
                }               
                
                $(document).ready(function(){
                    $("#BVVipPoint").draggable();
                })
            </script>

<script>

    var CheckSound = function (setter) {

        var soundCheck = localStorage.getItem('enableSound');
        if (setter != undefined) {
            localStorage.setItem('enableSound', (soundCheck == undefined || soundCheck == 0) ? 1 : 0);
        }
        soundCheck = localStorage.getItem('enableSound');
        if (soundCheck == undefined || soundCheck == 0) {
            $(".sound i").removeClass("fa-volume-up");
            $(".sound i").addClass("fa-volume-off");
            App.backgroundSound.stop();
        } else {
            $(".sound i").removeClass("fa-volume-off");
            $(".sound i").addClass("fa-volume-up");
            App.backgroundSound.setLoop(9999);
            App.backgroundSound.play();
        }
    }


</script>
<div id="penaltyBounder" style="width:1000px;margin: 0 auto; display:block">
    <div class="wrap" id="penaltyWrap">
        <a onclick="CheckSound(true);" class="sound"><i class="fa fa-volume-off fa-2x"></i></a>

<script type="text/javascript">
    var firstTimeShowJp = 1;
    var allowUpdateJpList = 0;
    $(document).ready(function(){
        setTimeout(function(){
            if(firstTimeShowJp == 0){
                allowUpdateJpList = 1;
            }
        },5)
        if(jpGetListInteval){
            clearInterval(jpGetListInteval);
        }
        jpGetListInteval = setInterval(function () {
            if(allowUpdateJpList > 0){
                UpdateJackpotList();
            }
        }, 7000);

        $('#event_qhlobby').click(function(){
            if($(this).hasClass('effect_qhlobby')){
                $(this).removeClass('effect_qhlobby');
                $('.quyhoach-lobby').css('left', '-69px');
            }else{
                $('#husao_qhlobby').removeClass('effect_qhlobby');
                $(this).addClass('effect_qhlobby');
                $('.quyhoach-lobby').css('left', '-39px');
            }
            if($('.eventall').hasClass('show_active')){
                $('.eventall').removeClass('show_active');
            }else{
                $('.eventall').addClass('show_active');
            }
            if($('#listGameJackpot').hasClass('show_active')){
                $('ul.phong').removeClass('show_active');
                $('#listGameJackpot').removeClass('show_active');
                sessionStorage.removeItem('showActive');
            }
        });

        $('#event_qhlobby').one('mouseenter', function() {
            if(!sessionStorage.getItem('firstEventHover')){
                $('#husao_qhlobby').removeClass('effect_qhlobby');
                $('ul.phong').removeClass('show_active');
                $('#listGameJackpot').removeClass('show_active');
            }

            if(sessionStorage.getItem('firstEventHover')){
                console.log('okevent');
            }else{
                $(this).addClass('effect_qhlobby');
                $('.eventall').addClass('show_active');
                $('.quyhoach-lobby').css('left', '-39px');
            }
            sessionStorage.setItem('firstEventHover', true);
        });
        /*
        $('#husao_qhlobby').one('mouseenter', function() {
            if(sessionStorage.getItem('firstEventHover')){
                $('#event_qhlobby').removeClass('effect_qhlobby');
                $('.eventall').removeClass('show_active');
            }

            if(sessionStorage.getItem('firstHusaoHover')){
                console.log('okhusao');
            }else{
                $(this).addClass('effect_qhlobby');
                $('ul.phong').addClass('show_active');
                $('#listGameJackpot').addClass('show_active');
                $('.quyhoach-lobby').css('left', '-39px');
            }
            sessionStorage.setItem('showActive', true);
            sessionStorage.setItem('firstHusaoHover', true);
        });
        */
        $('#husao_qhlobby').click(function(){
            if($(this).hasClass('effect_qhlobby')){
                $(this).removeClass('effect_qhlobby');
                $('.quyhoach-lobby').css('left', '-69px');
            }else{
                $('#event_qhlobby').removeClass('effect_qhlobby');
                $(this).addClass('effect_qhlobby');
                $('.quyhoach-lobby').css('left', '-39px');
            }
            if($('.eventall').hasClass('show_active')){
                $('.eventall').removeClass('show_active');
            }
            if($('#listGameJackpot').hasClass('show_active')){
                $('ul.phong').removeClass('show_active');
                $('#listGameJackpot').removeClass('show_active');
                sessionStorage.removeItem('showActive');
            }else{
                $('ul.phong').addClass('show_active');
                $('#listGameJackpot').addClass('show_active');
                sessionStorage.setItem('showActive', true);
            }
        });
    });

    function openLhs_minipoker()
    {
        if (!App.currentAccount || !(App.currentAccount.AccountID > 0)) {
            $("#btn_login").click();
            return;
        }
        var betValue = 10000;
        if ($('#slotmachine').css('display') == 'none')
        {
            commonGame.showhide(2);
        }
        if(betValue == 100) commonSlot.setPriceBet(1);
        if(betValue == 1000) commonSlot.setPriceBet(2);
        if(betValue == 10000) commonSlot.setPriceBet(3);
    }

    function openLhs_minivuabai() {
        if (!App.currentAccount || !(App.currentAccount.AccountID > 0)) {
            $("#btn_login").click();
            return;
        }
        var betValue = 10000;
        if ($("#miniVuabai").is(":visible") == false)
        {
            commonGame.showhide(4);
            setTimeout(function(){
                if(betValue == 100) miniVuabai.chontien(100);
                if(betValue == 1000) miniVuabai.chontien(1000);
                if(betValue == 10000) miniVuabai.chontien(10000);
                $("#tien100").removeClass("chon");
                $("#tien1000").removeClass("chon");
                $("#tien5000").removeClass("chon");
                $("#tien10000").removeClass("chon");
                $("#tien10000").addClass("chon")
            },1000);
        }
    }

    function UpdateJackpotList() {
        if($('#listGameJackpot').hasClass('show_active'))
        {
            $.ajax({
                type: "GET",
                url: "http://vuachoibai.com/event//Jackpot/GetJsonJackpotList?betValue=10000",
                success: function (data) {

                    $("#listGameJackpot").html("");

                    //update new element
                    data = JSON.parse(data);
                    for (var i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
                        if ($("#GameLi_" + data[i].GameIcon).html() == undefined)//non-exist element
                        {
                            var strElement = '';

                            if(sessionStorage.getItem('MoneyValue_' + data[i].GameIcon)){
                                var firstNumber = sessionStorage.getItem('MoneyValue_' + data[i].GameIcon);
                                var jackpotNumber = firstNumber;
                            }else{
                                var jackpotNumber = data[i].Jackpot - 100000;
                            }     

                           
                            if (data[i].GameIcon == "chuadao") {
                                strElement = '<li id="GameLi_' + data[i].GameIcon + '">';
                                strElement += '<div>';
                                strElement += '<img src="http://vuachoibai.com/event//Contents/ListJackpot/icon/' + data[i].GameIcon + '.png">';
                                strElement += '<span>';
                                if(data[i].NotIsAdv > 0){
                                    if(data[i].IsEvent > 0){
                                        strElement += '<img src="http://vuachoibai.com/event//Contents/ListJackpot/tophu_event.png">';
                                    }else{
                                        strElement += '<img src="http://vuachoibai.com/event//Contents/ListJackpot/tophu_qc.png">';
                                    }
                                }else{
                                    if(data[i].IsEvent > 0){
                                        strElement += '<img src="http://vuachoibai.com/event//Contents/ListJackpot/tophu_event.png">';
                                    }else{
                                        strElement += '<img src="http://vuachoibai.com/event//Contents/ListJackpot/tophu_qc.png">';
                                    }
                                }
                                strElement += '</span>';
                                strElement += '</div>';
                                strElement += '<a href="'+ data[i].GameUrl +'" target="_blank">';
                                strElement += '<div>';
                                strElement += '<h4>Tam quốc xèng/ Chúa đảo</h4>';
                                strElement += '<p>';
                                strElement += '<img src="http://vuachoibai.com/event//Contents/ListJackpot/top_hu_tien.png">';
                                strElement += '<unknowtag id="MoneyValue_' + data[i].GameIcon + '">' + jackpotNumber.toString() + '</unknowtag>';
                                strElement += '</p>';
                                strElement += '</div>';
                                strElement += '</a>';
                                strElement += '<div class="sub-phong">';
                                strElement += '<ul>';
                                strElement += '<li><a href="http://vuachoibai.com/tam-quoc-xeng/?utm_source=wcgdg&utm_medium=listhu&utm_term=cgdg&utm_content=f&utm_campaign=CGDG" target="_blank">Tam Quốc Xèng</a></li>';
                                strElement += '<li><a href="http://phatloc.vtcgame.vn/chua-dao?utm_source=wcgdg&utm_medium=listhu&utm_term=cgdg&utm_content=f&utm_campaign=CGDG" target="_blank">Chúa đảo</a></li>';
                                strElement += '<ul>';
                                strElement += '</div>';
                                strElement += '</li>';
                            } else {
                                strElement = '<li id="GameLi_' + data[i].GameIcon + '">';
                                strElement += '<div>';
                                strElement += '<img src="http://vuachoibai.com/event//Contents/ListJackpot/icon/' + data[i].GameIcon + '.png">';
                                strElement += '<span>';
                                if(data[i].NotIsAdv > 0){
                                    if(data[i].IsEvent > 0){
                                        strElement += '<img src="http://vuachoibai.com/event//Contents/ListJackpot/tophu_event.png">';
                                    }else{
                                        strElement += '<img src="http://vuachoibai.com/event//Contents/ListJackpot/tophu_qc.png">';
                                    }
                                }else{
                                    if(data[i].GameIcon == "dechesao"){
                                        strElement += '<img src="http://vuachoibai.com/event//Contents/ListJackpot/tophu_new.png">';
                                    }else{
                                        strElement += '<img src="http://vuachoibai.com/event//Contents/ListJackpot/tophu_qc.png">';
                                    }
                                }
                                strElement += '</span>';
                                strElement += '</div>';
                                if (data[i].DirectOpen == 1) {
                                    strElement += '<a href="javascript:void(0);" onclick="openLhs_' + data[i].GameIcon + '()">';
                                    strElement += '<div>';
                                    strElement += '<h4>' + data[i].GameName + '</h4>';
                                    strElement += '<p>';
                                    strElement += '<img src="http://vuachoibai.com/event//Contents/ListJackpot/top_hu_tien.png">';
                                    strElement += '<unknowtag id="MoneyValue_' + data[i].GameIcon + '">' + jackpotNumber.toString() + '</unknowtag>';
                                    strElement += '</p>';
                                    strElement += '</div>';
                                    strElement += '</a>';
                                }else{
                                    strElement += '<a href="' + data[i].GameUrl + '" target="_blank">';
                                    strElement += '<div>';
                                    strElement += '<h4>' + data[i].GameName + '</h4>';
                                    strElement += '<p>';
                                    strElement += '<img src="http://vuachoibai.com/event//Contents/ListJackpot/top_hu_tien.png">';
                                    strElement += '<unknowtag id="MoneyValue_' + data[i].GameIcon + '">' + jackpotNumber.toString() + '</unknowtag>';
                                    strElement += '</p>';
                                    strElement += '</div>';
                                    strElement += '</a>';
                                }
                                strElement += '</li>';
                            }
                            $("#listGameJackpot").append(strElement);
                        }

                        $("#GameLi_" + data[i].GameIcon).appendTo($("#listGameJackpot"));
                        var options = {
                            useEasing: true,
                            useGrouping: true,
                            separator: '.',
                            decimal: '.',
                            prefix: '',
                            suffix: ''
                        };

                        sessionStorage.setItem('MoneyValue_' + data[i].GameIcon, data[i].Jackpot);

                        if ($("#MoneyValue_" + data[i].GameIcon).html().replace(".", "") != data[i].Jackpot.toString()) {
                            var demo = new CountUp("MoneyValue_" + data[i].GameIcon, $("#MoneyValue_" + data[i].GameIcon).html().replace(/\./g, ""), data[i].Jackpot, 0, 4, options);
                            demo.start();
                        }else if(parseInt($("#MoneyValue_" + data[i].GameIcon).html().replace(/\./g, "")) == data[i].Jackpot){
                            var demo = new CountUp("MoneyValue_" + data[i].GameIcon, $("#MoneyValue_" + data[i].GameIcon).html().replace(/\./g, ""), data[i].Jackpot, 0, 4, options);
                            demo.start();
                        }
                    }
                    var html = '<div class="clear"></div>'
                                 + '<div class="bang-bieu">'
                                 + '<img src="http://vuachoibai.com/event//Contents/ListJackpot/images/bang_husao.png">'
